Your goal is to achieve a certain score to win the game.\r\nIn order to get the pieces (or tiles, or bones) together, the number of pips at the end of each of the tiles must match. It is that simple. The main difference is you have to pass your turn if you run out of options (whereas you can pick an extra domino from the boneyard in the previous mode).\r\n\r\n- Dominoes All Five: slightly more complex.
